1. merge data -

ShaRep_AIA_merge <- BBAIA %>% 
  left_join(ShaRep, by = c("YM" = "ym", "CIK" = "cik") ) %>% 
  filter(AIA >= 0 & AIA <= 5) %>% 
  filter(ShaRep3 < quantile(ShaRep3, probs = 0.9, na.rm = T)) %>%
  na.omit() 
  # mutate(ShaRep3 = format(ShaRep3, scientific = FALSE))
# ShaRep_AIA_merge %>% head(300) %>% View()
# names(ShaRep_AIA_merge)
